<h1 class="header"> <span class="itemprop" itemprop="name">Elvis Presley</span>
<span>(1935–1977)</span>
</h1>
<div class="infobar" id="name-job-categories">
<a href="#soundtrack" onclick="nameJobCategoriesClickHandler(this)"> <span class="itemprop" itemprop="jobTitle">
Soundtrack</span></a> <span class="ghost">|</span>
<a href="#actor" onclick="nameJobCategoriesClickHandler(this)"> <span class="itemprop" itemprop="jobTitle">
Actor</span></a> <span class="ghost">|</span>
<a href="#music_department" onclick="nameJobCategoriesClickHandler(this)"> <span class="itemprop" itemprop="jobTitle">
Music Department</span></a>
</div>
<hr/>
<div class="txt-block" id="name-bio-text">
<div class="name-trivia-bio-text">
<div class="inline" itemprop="description">
Elvis Aaron Presley was born on January 8, 1935 in East Tupelo, Mississippi.He had a twin brother that was a still born. In September 1948 when Elvis was 13, he and his parents moved to Memphis, Tennessee where he attended Humes Highschool. In 1953 Elvis attended the senior prom with the current girl he was courting, Regis Wilson. After graduating...            <span class="see-more inline nobr-only">
<a href="/name/nm0000062/bio?ref_=nm_ov_bio_sm">See full bio</a> »
            </span>
</div> </div>
</div>
<div class="txt-block" id="name-born-info">
<h4 class="inline">Born:</h4>
<a href="/name/nm0000062/bio?ref_=nm_ov_bth_nm"> Elvis Aron Presley
</a> <br/>
<time datetime="1935-1-8" itemprop="birthDate">
<a href="/search/name?birth_monthday=1-8&amp;refine=birth_monthday&amp;ref_=nm_ov_bth_monthday">January 8</a>, 
     
<a href="/search/name?birth_year=1935&amp;ref_=nm_ov_bth_year">1935</a>
</time>
            in
            <a href="/search/name?birth_place=Tupelo%2C+Mississippi%2C+USA&amp;ref_=nm_ov_bth_place">Tupelo, Mississippi, USA</a>
</div>
<div class="txt-block" id="name-death-info">
<h4 class="inline">Died:</h4>
<time datetime="1977-8-16" itemprop="deathDate">
<a href="/search/name?death_monthday=8-16&amp;refine=death_monthday&amp;ref_=nm_ov_dth_monthday">August 16</a>, 
     
<a href="/search/name?death_date=1977&amp;ref_=nm_ov_dth_year">1977</a>
</time>
         (age 42) 
         in <a href="/search/name?death_place=Memphis%2C+Tennessee%2C+USA&amp;ref_=nm_ov_dth_place">Memphis, Tennessee, USA</a>
</div>
</td>

</td>

                    »
        </div>
<hr/>
<div class="see-more inline canwrap" id="dyk-trivia">
<h4 class="inline">Trivia:</h4>
When <a href="/name/nm0838047?ref_=nm_dyk_trv1">Ed Sullivan</a> finally allowed him to appear on <a href="/title/tt0040053?ref_=nm_dyk_trv2">The Ed Sullivan Show</a> (1948), he was filmed from the waist upwards only once, on his third and final appearance on Sunday, January 6th, 1957.                    <span class="see-more inline">
<a href="/name/nm0000062/bio?ref_=nm_dyk_trv_sm#trivia">See more</a>
</span>
                    »
        </div>
